TUR_remove_add_dynamic_modifiers = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_national_economy } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_national_economy }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_national_economy }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_agrarian_economy } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_agrarian_economy }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_agrarian_economy }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_second_constitutional_era } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_second_constitutional_era }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_second_constitutional_era }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_a_bygone_era } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_a_bygone_era }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_a_bygone_era }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_the_modern_era } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_the_modern_era }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_the_modern_era }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_ottoman_navy } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_ottoman_navy }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_ottoman_navy }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_havacilik_komisyonu } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_havacilik_komisyonu }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_havacilik_komisyonu }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_separatist_sentiments } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_separatist_sentiments }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_separatist_sentiments }
		}
	}
}

TUR_remove_current_sultan = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_abdulhamid_ii
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_abdulhamid_ii
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = HJZ_hussein_bin_ali_caliph
		}
		remove_ideas = HJZ_hussein_bin_ali_caliph
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_vi
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_vi
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_abdulmecid_ii
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_abdulmecid_ii
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_ahmed_nihad
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_ahmed_nihad
	}
}
TUR_increase_literacy = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_1
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_2
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_3
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_4
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_5
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_6
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_7
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_8
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_9
				has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_10
			}
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_encouraged_education_1
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_1
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_2
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_3
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_4
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_4
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_5
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_5
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_6
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_6
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_6
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_7
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_7
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_7
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_8
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_8
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_8
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_9
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_9
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_9
			add_idea = TUR_encouraged_education_10
		}
	}
}
TUR_balkan_economy_level_up = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_5
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_5
			add_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_6
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_4
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_4
			add_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_5
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_3
			add_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_4
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_2
			add_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_3
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_1
			add_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_1
		}
			add_ideas = TUR_idea_balkan_economic_sphere_1
	}
}

TUR_minority_revolt_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = TUR
			any_controlled_state = { resistance > 79 }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				resistance > 79.9
				is_owned_by = TUR
			}
			controller = { country_event = ottoman.0 }
		}
	}
}

TUR_minority_generic_add_manpower_stability_war_support_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor < 0 } }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor
			max = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_stability_factor < 0 } }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_stability_factor = 0.002 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_state_stability_factor
			max = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_war_support_factor < 0 } }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_war_support_factor = 0.001 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_state_war_support_factor
			max = 0
		}
	}
}

TUR_add_armenian_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level > 0 } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_armenian_state
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = TUR } }
			set_state_flag = TUR_armenian_no_control
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_controlled_by = TUR }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
		}
	}
}
TUR_add_greek_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level > 0 } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_greek_state
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = TUR } }
			set_state_flag = TUR_greek_no_control
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_controlled_by = TUR }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
		}
	}
}

TUR_add_azerbaijani_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_azerbaijani_state_level > 0 } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_azerbaijani_state
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = TUR } }
			set_state_flag = TUR_azerbaijani_no_control
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_controlled_by = TUR }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_azerbaijani_minority }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { compliance < 30 }
					set_compliance = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

TUR_remove_armenian_effect = {
	hidden_effect = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority } }
	clr_state_flag = TUR_armenian_state
	add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition = -0.05 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = TUR_ottoman_attrition
		min = 0
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor = 0.05 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor
		max = 0
	}
	set_variable = { TUR_minority_enemy_local_supplies_down = 0 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = TUR_minority_enemy_local_supplies_down
		min = 0
	}
	TUR_minority_generic_add_manpower_stability_war_support_effect = yes
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_armenian_to_greek_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_greek_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_armenian_to_jewish_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_jewish_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_jewish_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_armenian_to_south_slavic_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_south_slavic_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_south_slavic_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_armenian_to_albanian_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_albanian_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_armenian_to_kurdish_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_kurdish_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_kurdish_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_armenian_to_arab_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_arab_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_assyrian_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_armenian_to_assyrian_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_assyrian_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_assyrian_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_georgian_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_armenian_to_georgian_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_georgian_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_romanian_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_armenian_to_romanian_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_romanian_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_azerbaijani_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_armenian_to_azerbaijani_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_azerbaijani_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_azerbaijani_state
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { compliance < 30 }
				set_compliance = 30
			}
		}
	}
	else = { effect_tooltip = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority } } }
}

TUR_remove_greek_effect = {
	hidden_effect = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority } }
	clr_state_flag = TUR_greek_state
	add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies = -0.1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies
		min = 0
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor = -0.02 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor
		min = 0
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_factories = 0.05 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = TUR_ottoman_local_factories
		max = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			state = 757
			check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_state_level > 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor = 0.025 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor
				max = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_stability_factor < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_stability_factor = 0.001 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = TUR_ottoman_state_stability_factor
				max = 0
			}
		}
	}
	else = { TUR_minority_generic_add_manpower_stability_war_support_effect = yes }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_greek_to_armenian_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_armenian_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_greek_to_jewish_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_jewish_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_jewish_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_greek_to_south_slavic_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_south_slavic_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_south_slavic_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_greek_to_albanian_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_albanian_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_greek_to_kurdish_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_kurdish_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_kurdish_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_greek_to_arab_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_arab_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_assyrian_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_greek_to_assyrian_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_assyrian_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_assyrian_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_georgian_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_greek_to_georgian_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_georgian_state
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_romanian_state_level > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_greek_to_romanian_minority
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority } }
		set_state_flag = TUR_romanian_state
	}
	else_if = {

TUR_domestic_weapon_research_tank = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = TUR_domestic_weapon_companies
			has_idea = tulomsas
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_attack_factor < 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_defence_factor < 0 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_domestic_weapon_research_tt
			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_attack_factor = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_defence_factor = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_attack_factor_tt = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_defence_factor_tt = -0.005 }
		}
	}
}

ottoman_minority_variable_check = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_controlled_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_stability_factor = -0.01 }
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			#country_event = { id = ottoman.100 days = 4 }
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor = 0 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_subject_vilayet = yes
				has_variable = TUR_armenian_state_level
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = -0.01 }
			set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = -0.01 }
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_revive_the_ottomanism_dream } }
				add_to_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 0.002 }
				add_to_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 0.002 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level = 1 } }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level = 2 } }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 2 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 2 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level = 3 } }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor = 3 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level = 4 } }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
				divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 4 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 4 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor = 4 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
			add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor }
			add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor = TUR_armenian_population_political_power_factor }
		}
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_341_population_stability_factor = 341.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_347_population_stability_factor = 347.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_1019_population_stability_factor = 1019.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_825_population_stability_factor = 825.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_349_population_stability_factor = 349.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_348_population_stability_factor = 348.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_344_population_stability_factor = 344.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_857_population_stability_factor = 857.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_881_population_stability_factor = 881.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_350_population_stability_factor = 350.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_352_population_stability_factor = 352.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_353_population_stability_factor = 353.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_806_population_stability_factor = 806.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_816_population_stability_factor = 816.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }

		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_938_population_stability_factor = 938.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_818_population_stability_factor = 818.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }

TUR_state_remove_specific_minority_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
				has_state_flag = TUR_removed_armenian_state
			}
		}
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
		clr_state_flag = TUR_armenian_state
		clr_state_flag = TUR_armenian_state_no_control
		set_state_flag = TUR_removed_armenian_state
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
				has_state_flag = TUR_removed_arab_state
			}
		}
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
		clr_state_flag = TUR_arab_state
		clr_state_flag = TUR_arab_state_no_control
		set_state_flag = TUR_removed_arab_state
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
				has_state_flag = TUR_removed_greek_state
			}
		}
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
		clr_state_flag = TUR_greek_state
		clr_state_flag = TUR_greek_state_no_control
		set_state_flag = TUR_removed_greek_state
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_south_slavic_minority }
				has_state_flag = TUR_removed_south_slavic_state
			}
		}
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_south_slavic_minority }
		clr_state_flag = TUR_south_slavic_state
		clr_state_flag = TUR_south_slavic_state_no_control
		set_state_flag = TUR_removed_south_slavic_state
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority }
				has_state_flag = TUR_removed_albanian_state
			}
		}
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority }
		clr_state_flag = TUR_albanian_state
		clr_state_flag = TUR_albanian_state_no_control
		set_state_flag = TUR_removed_albanian_state
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_kurdish_minority }
				has_state_flag = TUR_removed_kurd_state
			}
		}
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_kurdish_minority }
		clr_state_flag = TUR_kurdish_state
		clr_state_flag = TUR_kurdish_state_no_control
		set_state_flag = TUR_removed_kurd_state
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
				has_state_flag = TUR_removed_georgian_state
			}
		}
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
		clr_state_flag = TUR_georgian_state
		clr_state_flag = TUR_georgian_state_no_control
		set_state_flag = TUR_removed_georgian_state
	}
	if = {

TUR_debt_value_check = {
    hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1 = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1_opposite = 0 }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods < 0 } }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1 = -0.01 }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1_opposite = 0.01 }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1 = -0.01 } }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1_opposite = 0.01 } }
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_1 = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_1_opposite = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2 = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_opposite = 0 }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.01 } }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2 = -0.01 }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_opposite = 0.01 }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_1 = -0.01 } }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_1_opposite = 0.01 } }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods < -0.01 } }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2 = -0.02 }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_opposite = 0.02 }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2 = -0.02 } }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_opposite = 0.02 } }
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2 = TUR_has_debt_2_1 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_opposite = TUR_has_debt_2_1_opposite }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_3_1 = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_3_1_opposite = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_3_2 = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_3_2_opposite = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_3 = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_3_opposite = 0 }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.01 } }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2 = -0.01 }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_opposite = 0.01 }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_1 = -0.01 } }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_1_opposite = 0.01 } }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.02 } }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_3 = -0.02 }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_3_opposite = 0.02 }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_3_1 = -0.02 } }

TUR_remove_debt_1_FROM = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_1
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.01 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_FROM
		}
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.01 }
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = 0.01 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods
			min = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.01 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_FROM
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_1_FROM }
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = 0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = -0.01 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods
					max = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_debt_value_check = yes
}

			add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = 0.05 }

		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods
			min = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { any_other_country = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = opda_consumer_goods
				check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods < 0 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_1_ALL
			custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
			add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = 0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = -0.01 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = opda_consumer_goods
				max = 0
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_debt_value_check = yes
}

	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_2
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.02 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_FROM
		}
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.02 }
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = 0.02 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods
			min = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.02 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_FROM
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_2_FROM }
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = 0.02 }
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = -0.02 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods
					max = 0
				}
			}
		}

			limit = { FROM = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.03 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_FROM
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_3_FROM }
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = 0.03 }
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = -0.03 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods
					max = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}

		limit = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_8
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.08 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_ITA
		}
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.08 }
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = 0.08 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods
			min = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ITA = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.08 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_ITA
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_8_ITA }
		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = 0.08 }
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = -0.08 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods
					max = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_debt_value_check = yes
}

TUR_anatolian_grain_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_2
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_3
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_3 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_3
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_4
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_4 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_4
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_5
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_5 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_5
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_6
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_6 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_6
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_7
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_7 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_7
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_8
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_8 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_8
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_9
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_9 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_9
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_10
		}
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_utilize_anatolian_grain_var = 1 }
}

TUR_reduce_naval_blockade = {
	add_to_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade = -1 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_20
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_19
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_18
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_17
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_16
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_15
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_14
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_13
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_12
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_11
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_10
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_9
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_8
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_7
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_6
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_5
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_4
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_3
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_2
				has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 1 } }
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_20
					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_19
				}
			}
		}
		else = { effect_tooltip = { remove_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade_1 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_20 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_20
					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_19
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_19 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_19
					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_18
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_18 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_18
					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_17
				}
			}
			else_if = {

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_17
					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_16
				}
			}
			else_if = {

					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_14
				}
			}
			else_if = {

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_7
					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_6
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_6 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_6
					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_5 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_5
					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_4 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_4
					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_3
					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_2
					add_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade_1 }
				remove_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade_1
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_state_development_category = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = wasteland }
		set_state_category = pastoral
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = enclave }
		set_state_category = pastoral
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = tiny_island }
		set_state_category = small_island
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = pastoral }
		set_state_category = rural
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = small_island }
		set_state_category = rural
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = rural }
		set_state_category = town
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = town }
		set_state_category = large_town
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = large_town }
		set_state_category = city
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = city }
		set_state_category = large_city
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = large_city }
		set_state_category = metropolis
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = metropolis }
		set_state_category = megalopolis
	}
}

			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_experience_gain_army_factor = -0.1 }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_max_planning = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_power = 2 }
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 2 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_experience_gain_army_factor = -0.05 }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_stability_factor = -0.025 }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_max_planning = -0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_power = 2 }
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 1 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_experience_gain_army_factor = -0.05 }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_stability_factor = -0.05 }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_max_planning = -0.1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_power = 1 }
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 5 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_political_power_gain = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_power = 1 }
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 4 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_political_power_gain = 0.02 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_power = 1 }
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 3 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_planning_speed = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_power = 1 }
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 2 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_foreign_subversive_activites = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_power = 1 }
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 1 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_itilafist_foreign_subversive_activites = 0.15 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_af_experience_gain_army_factor = TUR_itilafist_experience_gain_army_factor }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_af_army_morale_factor = TUR_itilafist_army_morale_factor }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_af_stability_factor = TUR_itilafist_stability_factor }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_af_planning_speed = TUR_itilafist_planning_speed }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_af_max_planning = TUR_itilafist_max_planning }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_af_command_power_gain_mult = TUR_itilafist_command_power_gain_mult }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_af_political_power_gain = TUR_itilafist_political_power_gain }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_af_foreign_subversive_activites = TUR_itilafist_foreign_subversive_activites }
		#
		set_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = neutrality
					has_government = fascism
					has_government = communism
				}
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ahmed_muhtar } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_mehmed_v } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_abdulhamid_ii } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_mehmed_vi } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_abdulmecid_ii } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ahmed_nihad } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_osman_iv } }
			}
			add_to_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = TUR_ittihadist_loyalty }
			subtract_from_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = TUR_itilafist_loyalty }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = TUR_ittihadist_power }
			subtract_from_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = TUR_itilafist_power }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = democratic
					has_government = communism
					has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ahmed_muhtar }
					has_country_leader = { character = TUR_mehmed_v }
					has_country_leader = { character = TUR_abdulhamid_ii }
					has_country_leader = { character = TUR_mehmed_vi }
					has_country_leader = { character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin }
					has_country_leader = { character = TUR_abdulmecid_ii }
					has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ahmed_nihad }
					has_country_leader = { character = TUR_osman_iv }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = TUR_itilafist_loyalty }
			subtract_from_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = TUR_ittihadist_loyalty }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = TUR_itilafist_power }
			subtract_from_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = TUR_ittihadist_power }
		}
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_powerful_loyal }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_powerful_neutral }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_powerful_disloyal }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_extended_power_loyal }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_extended_power_neutral }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_extended_power_disloyal }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_limited_power_loyal }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_limited_power_neutral }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_limited_power_disloyal }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_decreased_power_loyal }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_decreased_power_neutral }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_decreased_power_disloyal }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_minimal_power_loyal }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_minimal_power_neutral }
		remove_ideas = { modifier = TUR_army_factionalism_minimal_power_disloyal }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 4 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 2 }
				}
				check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 4 }
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_powerful_loyal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 1 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 0 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -1 }
				}
				check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 4 }
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_powerful_neutral
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -2 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -4 }
				}
				check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 4 }
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_powerful_disloyal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 4 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 2 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 2 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_extended_power_loyal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 1 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 0 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -1 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 2 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_extended_power_neutral
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -2 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -4 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 2 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_extended_power_disloyal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 4 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 2 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 1 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 0 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_limited_power_loyal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 1 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 0 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -1 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 1 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 0 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_limited_power_neutral
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -2 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -4 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 1 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = 0 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_limited_power_disloyal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 4 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 2 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -1 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -2 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_decreased_power_loyal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 1 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 0 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -1 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -1 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -2 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_decreased_power_neutral
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -2 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -4 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -1 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -2 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_decreased_power_disloyal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 4 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 2 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -4 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_minimal_power_loyal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 1 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = 0 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -1 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -4 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_minimal_power_neutral
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -2 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_loyalty = -4 }
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -3 }
					check_variable = { TUR_army_factionalism_icon_power = -4 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas =TUR_army_factionalism_minimal_power_disloyal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty < 2 }
				check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power > 2 }
				has_completed_focus = TUR_appoint_the_opposition
			}
			activate_mission = TUR_action_army_coup
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty < 2 }
				check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power > 2 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_action_army_coup }
				has_country_flag = TUR_saviour_officer_coup
			}
			activate_mission = TUR_raid_on_the_sublime_porte
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty < 2 }
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_power > 3 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_saviour_officer_coup }
			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_saviour_officer_organized
			activate_mission = TUR_saviour_officer_coup
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty < 2 }
				check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_power > 3 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_saviour_officer_coup }
				has_country_flag = TUR_action_army_coup
			}
			activate_mission = TUR_march_on_harbiye_nezareti
		}
	}
}
TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = 5 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty_tt_loyal
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = 4 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty_tt_loyal
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = 3 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty_tt_friendly
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = 2 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty_tt_neutral
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = 1 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty_tt_opposed
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = 1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = TUR_ittihadist_loyalty
		min = 1
		max = 5
	}
	TUR_add_appropriate_army_factionalism_icon = yes
}
TUR_decrease_ittihadist_loyalty = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = 5 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty_tt_friendly
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = 4 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty_tt_neutral
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = 3 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty_tt_opposed
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = 2 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty_tt_hostile
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = 1 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty_tt_hostile
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty = -1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = TUR_ittihadist_loyalty
		min = 1
		max = 5
	}
	TUR_add_appropriate_army_factionalism_icon = yes
}
TUR_increase_ittihadist_power = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = 5 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_power_tt_powerful
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = 4 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_power_tt_powerful
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = 3 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_power_tt_extended
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = 2 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_power_tt_limited
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = 1 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_power_tt_decreased
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = 1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = TUR_ittihadist_power
		min = 1
		max = 5
	}
	TUR_add_appropriate_army_factionalism_icon = yes
}
TUR_decrease_ittihadist_power = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = 5 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_power_tt_extended
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = 4 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_power_tt_limited
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = 3 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_power_tt_decreased
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = 2 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_power_tt_minimal
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = 1 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_ittihadist_power_tt_minimal
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power = -1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = TUR_ittihadist_power
		min = 1
		max = 5
	}
	TUR_add_appropriate_army_factionalism_icon = yes
}

		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 5 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_itilafist_loyalty_tt_loyal
	}
	else_if = {

	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 3 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_itilafist_loyalty_tt_friendly

		var = TUR_itilafist_loyalty
		min = 1
		max = 5
	}
	TUR_add_appropriate_army_factionalism_icon = yes
}
TUR_decrease_itilafist_loyalty = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 5 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_itilafist_loyalty_tt_friendly
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 4 } }

		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_itilafist_loyalty = 3 } }

		max = 5

}

TUR_liberation_war_defeat_effect = {
	FROM = { white_peace = ROOT }
	if = {
		limit = {
			ENG = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
		}
		ENG = { puppet = TUR }
	}
	set_cosmetic_tag = TUR_Sultanate
	if = {
		limit = {
			GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_venizelos_tittoni_agreement }
			ITA = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
		}
		824 = { transfer_state_to = ITA }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			SOV = {
				exists = no
			}
			RUS = {
				exists = yes
				has_country_flag = great_war_winner
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			transfer_state = 352
			transfer_state = 353
			transfer_state = 806
		}
		else = {
			ARM = {
				transfer_state = 352
				transfer_state = 353
				transfer_state = 806
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			GRE = { has_country_flag = pontus_rebellion }
		}
		PON = {
			transfer_state = 354
			transfer_state = 355
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ARM = {
						owns_state = 353
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 354
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			GRE = {
				has_country_flag = pontus_confederation
			}
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		ARM = {
			annex_country = {
				target = PON
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PON
				}
				remove_core_of = PON
				add_core_of = ARM
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = PONARM
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FRA = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
		}
		TUR = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 344
						state = 857
						state = 829
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = FRA
			}					
		}
	}
	release = KUR
}

TRS_increase_arab_opposition = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_0 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_0
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_1 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_1
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_2
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_3 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_3
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_4 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_4
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_5 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_5
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_6
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_6 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_6
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_7
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_7 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_7
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_8
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_8 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_8
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_9
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_9 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_9
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_10
		}
	}
	else = { add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.03 } }
}

TRS_decrease_arab_opposition = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_10 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_10
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_9
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_9 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_9
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_8
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_8 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_8
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_7
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_7 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_7
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_6
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_6 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_6
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_5 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_5
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_4 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_4
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_3 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_3
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_2
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_1 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_1
			add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_0
		}
	}
	else = { add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = -0.03 } }
}
